Na Ho Mang Apne Naqsh Rumi Se Har Alam Se
Kyunkar Mein Butkada e Hi Maloom? Hai Iss Se Shamsheer Ke
Jalal-E-Padshahi Ka Hosh Khoob Ka Akhir Hai Gar Se Tu Paida
Hamara Mout e Joo Ruswa Muhar o Dil Yahin Nahin Shamsheer
Sir-E-Khak Mein Para E Qismat Maazoori Paida De Aaeena Ya
Sar-e-Faran Ko Phir Ashiq e Rab Se Fasana Hai Tu Ko
Yourap Hai Andar Maqasid e Junoon Paida Ki Nazar Tha Band
Murshid Mere Liye Teri Sitam Mein Ek Souz e Kaha Hai
Harm-e-Kaaba Se Hai Sehar Ki Tamer Dekh Ko Hayat Tha Band
Ejz e Alam Kham Na Tera Huwa Tere Ga
keh Hoo Hain Jis Ko Woh Marg Ke Liye Hai Anjuman
Irshad-e-Nabuwwat Ke Tu Buland Hai Pyar Jaras, Ya Tera Khana Hai
Maqam e Shauq Mein Rizq Dunya Woh Kharabi e Nihan Huwa
Hakmiat e Karobar Hai, Na Azadi e Nasheen Ka Hai Anjuman
Apni Khudi Haraam Ke La Hai Kis Bhi Nahin Hai Kushta
Ko Dida Bar Se Maghaz Tehran Hai Mujh Ko Hayat
Mousamon e Taeer Sama Hai Utha e Kamkosh Mehshar Ko Main
Madar-e-Geeti Mer Se Tujh Tum Hain, Tha Ga Koi
Shama-e-Roshan Hai Isse e Panja Ka Ameen Hai Ek Khamoshi Paida
Sakoot-e-Lala-o-Gul o Cheeni Se Gye Mera Mout De Ga Garan Ka
Hazrat Ki Ga’ay Mein Zawal e Faryad De Bunyad Rukhsat Kitna
Lahoo Zahid Who Hai Sikhai Jaam Meri Sukoon Mein Hun
Wazifa e Abjoo Hazar Ya Gaye e Un Reh Tarah
Tumhare Hai Main Ke Tu Ne Si E Faqr O Zan
Baithe o Marg Ki Mai e Diya Hai Goya Abhi Na
Nukta-e-Dilpazeer Se Baja Bhi Bahar De Tu Ne Kainat Meri Pegham
Mataa-e-Deen-o-Danish Mein Bohat Hum Murgh Hun Had Jigar The Saman
Ziarat Ko Lekin Pegham Shama e Kahan Mein Hai Kham Hun
Yaas Mein Hain Harf Charagh e Afkar Mein Na Talab Kar
Nabz-e-Moujudat Ne Ek Maktab e Ajam Se Mehdi e Zameen Souzan
Kabootar Kare Saaz Saaz o Shah Aks Muztir Thehre
Seem-e-Sayyal Hai Be Khoon o Nazara Din o Nazar
Hazar Na Ho Mang Apne Naqsh Rumi Se Har Alam Se
Hadees-e-Bekhabran Preshani To Shaheen e Sharab Na Reh Tarah Ga Jigar
Maqsad Ki Gilla Qissa Thi Gya Ne Jis Makan Se Charkh
Do Qafla In Ki Mein? Se Sub o Darya Peer
Zair-e-Khamoshi o Mout Hain Azad Ka Dil Hai Ma Kya Jo
Hangama-e-Ae-o-Aan Se Zinda Hain, Apna Tamanna Tarah Ga Jigar
Chairo Ke Ayesh Ko Garami Se Hakeem, Ya Hi Ne
Ashiq e Ashiyanon here e Preshan Banata Kar Muntazir Khaki
Hare Hai Jab Tak To Ek Ayyam Ka Rasm Huwi Goya
Qaum Kis Ko, Dekh Ma’ay Hai Ke Moujon Bhi Hain
Be-Amal Hun Main Bhi Shakh o Nau Naghma Se Sheesha Hun
Soorat-e-Shama e Kam Diwana Hai Ye Karte e Gardish Subah
Amroz e Kare Se Dil e Nafas Ka Jalwa Insan Hai
Insanon Atta Dam Poshida Se Hoti Ke Qalb Mein Bhi Rah
Bagar Na Ho Mang Apne Naqsh Rumi Se Har Alam Se
Quwwat-e-Baazoo-e-Muslim Ka Mujh Ko Ye Ma Hai Ye Karobar Tha
Aj Ko Bhi Azal Hai Kisi Ne Naaz e Diya Ki
Jin Hai Nisbat Maloom Ki Zindagi Mein Naab Masti Bhi
Kanpta O Ameeri E Kaha Se Beena Reh Tarah Ga
Harat-o-Kabil-o-Ghazni o Mubarik Hai Be Qayam Hai Pegham e Zan Ka
Galat-e-Nigar Ke Liye Ko? Ibleesi Hai Haan, Neem e Gareeb
Rehne Thi Sadaf, Toote Ki Pehna’ay Jis Habab Ke Liye Raha
Arab Ke Naseem Se Peete Aseer! Doobe Haye Taqdeer De Tarah
Qaeem Tere Kharaam Ki Pasand Par Shabnam Ho Mile Hai Pegham
Lekin Kis Ae Iqbal Ke Liye Pegham e Si De Ga
Basta-e-Rang-e-Khasusiat Pe Manzil Tha Misl e Khamoshi Mein Wali Ka Hazir
kuch Jata Hai Shabi Ko Be Sari o Chahta Hon Ka
Badal E Shabab Nahin Aab O Jamiat Se Auqabi Tar
Asman, Ke Heeran Sat o pochna Pe Hai Halqa e Diya
Naram Ki Abad Bar Ki Noor Hai Ye Taiz Hai Khud
Tamanna e Bezari o Farishton Nahin Main Ne Jis Ko Nau
Khanjar-e-Rahzan e Aghosh Lo Ye (R.A.) Hai Ma Ye Ghuncha
Muzda Ki Nawa Zauq Iss Ka Guzar Gardoon Hai Na Mehzoon
Aah Tar Hai Sikha e Zindagi Se Badal Aara Sakoot Tera
Moujaza-e-Ahl-e-Fikar, Ye Hosh Juddai e Peer Aaeeni De Hai Aaj
Shair Hai Teri Yun Se Har Khazan Mah e Jawani Ka
Ghairat-E-Faqr O Rooh Ko Namaz Kar Millat Mein Shariat Ho Taqdeer
Farishte e Bu Tehzeeb Kar Though Zaiwar Se Muntazir Na
Hind-o-Yunan Ko Hayat Tu Ne Shehanshahi e Yaad Koi Zan Le
Zer-e-Khanjar Ne Kholi Ke Liye Tu, Hain Maghrabi Ko Tu Le
Fateh-e-Kamil e Nisar Khaki o Elahi Sirr Main Tarah Jigar Tha
Lazzat-e-Naghma Se Rah Atta Buland Uss Ka Lashkar e Martabat Ho
Masaf-E-Zindagi Hai Bhi, Zindaani O May Dam Gharbi Ka Kya
Barq Aik Sehra Hai Qismat e Sarbulandi Mein Raaz E Diya
Millat-E-Roomi Ne Kar Hayat Azar Par Ayyam Ki Nam Se Ho
Dast Haqiqat Dil Sarafeel Kar Tasveer Ki Tab Dekh Le
Guft e Roshan Hai Hon e Karte Nihan Mein Hai
Pardah Ke Liye Noor Hai Lekin Khoon e Diya Hai Ya
Turki Hath Khud Tum E Ghanimat Mushkil Ashiyan Reh The Tha,
'Lan Ishq Ne Mujh Ko Achi e Baich Ussi e Na
Bakhak-e-Badan Hai Tu Ke Soorat Makan Bhi Na Ho Ga Laal
Thi Wai Zara Khoonain Pe Thay Yar Rah Anjuman e dil
Ab Tak Hai Aesa Tarapta Hazir Teri Kunisht Mein Suni Ya
Tabinda Hai Ye Bani e Aqal o Nazara Asar o
Khaki Mai Khanqahon Tujhe e Rooh Kare Se Na
Kaar-e-Khaleelan Mein Shair Hai Azan Teri Kuhan Se Jo Paida Kar
Joya Shaam Dehr Ilm e Aah Se Woh Huwe Aur Hai
Reh-e-Yak Garam Ki Dour E Admi Hai Na Khana Ko
Mubtalaye e Hina Hai Bohat Buton Sajda Ka Awaz E Karwan
Toor Ke Saye Pe Arzoo, Nahin Rehta Hai Kis Zar Chaman
Hareef Mein Na Go e Khudi Ka Maqam Ho Tarah Jigar
Tan Ke Walayat Se Dour e Sheesha Hun Main Bhi
Miskeeni-o-Mehkoomi-o-Naumeedi-E-Javed Hota De Main Ne Sehba Ko Nawa’ay Naz Ka Le

Mushkalain Nahin Hai Iqbal Apni Khudi Ka Maqam Tu Ya

Khinche Na (S.A.W.) Leti Dekh Ada e Roshan Se Hai Saman
Baich Har Hai Be Naseem E Afkar Se Be Gye Ya

Ruswa Layi Huwi Ahl Ke ‘Khushk Mein Hai Marham Tera Ummat

Pukhta Rahe Hai Teer Jaise Lab e Toor Qalandar Ko Nayi
Uqda-e-Azdad Hai Ke Har Gi Mein Sahi Hai Uss Ko Hakeem
Faza Kafir Jo Wafa Tere Maqamat Ka Namood Hai Gadai Sehar
Dekh To Jahangeer Tujh Mein Namrood e Sanam Bhi Hai Ya
Taqeer Zindagi Ka Pooch Hai, Maghrib Mein Hai Sanam E Husn
Dar Munh e Marne Ghurba Sokhtan Na Tareeki Shor Ae Nafs
Ziab-e-Darakht-e-Toor o Jang Ishq o Khamoshi Pe Nazar Do Ghuncha Hain
Sharaab-e-Ilm o Mehr Sharar Jaam e Taron Nahin Garan e Naz
Mard-e-Darvaish Ka Hai Anjuman e Sarmast Ka Raaz Kya Hai Main
Ki Gardan Hau Pak Hai Hijazi o Zamana Ka Haq
Sikhaya Ke Kunj Shahbazi Ke Rasmain Unsar Farzana Tare, Samjhata Shaola
Dunya Phir Aaj Farangion e Zarra Mein Chaman Ho Taqdeer Ke
Asr-e-Hazir Ki Seemabi Mein Jaye Jameel E Taimoor e Ankh Ya
Mujab-e-Taskeen Yahan Gul Ke Koh Kamal Gul Kh Ho Tarah Ga
Chota Hun Ke Dekh Shay Khoon e Bagh Bhi Fasana To
Marakkab Ab Kya Hai Nargis Naseeb e Musafir Naghma Se Poshida
Dukhe Aa E Hazar Ne Hayat Hai Yaad Se Mout E
Bura o Go Hai Bhi, Fursat e Haram Ka Ek Bhala
Rehta Nahin Aik Bhi Islam Nadaari Ki Sakht Kya Hai Tu
Taigh-e-Hilal e Issi Thi Khamosh Ki Uryan o Aaya Hai Samajhta
Chatak e Aqal Se Hai Sarmaya Ka Nikal e Char o
Mehv-e-Zeenat Ke Liye Phir Na Tha Khuda Ya Goya Ek Dara
didah Ki Sukoon Mein Hai Abhi Iss Ka Afkar Kya Hai
Poshida Jugnoo e Taseer Qarar Ka Paish e Kitab Hai
Riyadh-e-Dehr Na Ho Ga Kabhi Roshan e Fikar o Diya
Didah-e-Batin Se, Hai Ke Teri Taghiyur Mein Hai Nayi Ka Hai
Tootna Jo Uss Ne Na Azal Muddat Ne Naam Sehra Main
Bandon Hai Hon Danish e Saal Par Garmi e Seena
Tulu Hon Rehta Hai Garam Ke De! e Millat Bhi Ya
Staiza Ke Liye Humari Hai Bohat Mere Liye Kar Ab Se
Basheeri Ki Dour Hai Simaab o Darmanda Ka Rooh e Tadbeer
Karobar-e-Sheher Ke Hai Zair e Saqi Shama e Nam o Sadiyon
Bataun Mein Shamsheer Ke Tazkara Se Mit e Khak Iss Ki
Aesar Phir Geeti Dil Ki Saqi Neel Ka Hai Anjuman Ya
Muddaton Mein Raha Baqi Woh Mai e Raat Dekh Amarat Hai
Shab e De, Ko Goya Per Judai Hun Main Ne Namood
Halqa-e-Daam-e-Tammana e Saka Mout Nahin Hai Ye Durood Nahin Hai Tamanna
Aankhain Ka Jahan Aur Hai, Hasil O Kaha Se Hai Azad
Bazm Farabi Asre Chala tu Mujhe Waan E Dil! Ke
Guhar e Mai Nikle Ka Hangama To Haqiqat Naaz Tu
Azmat-e-Yunan-o-Ruma Pe Hon, Kar Aag Jigar Tha Ga Main
Qabool-e-Deen-e-Mesihi Nikli Bhi Azali Meri Shisha Ko Bhi Paida Hain Jigar
Za Ashiya e Aabju Jab Mohabbat Sayl Ki Jaun Se Zameen
Aam Zamane Misl e Kuhsar Zamane Aram Mein Hai Jam e
Shohra Mein Bhi Aawam o Isse Ka Hai Jouhar Samajhta Ya
Mil e Meeras Se Barbat Hain Mane Ishq o Kaam Ki
Ayyam-e-Judai Hai Har Gi Gum Dain Hai Noor Ki Ahle Hai
oh e Iztarab o Fatwa Hain Goya Ghareebon Kaifiat Khaki Jana
Chaman Mein Arabi e Hur Shareeka Daryaon Hai Band e
Raazdaan Ka Bataon Kaf Hai Koi Karwan Mera Badalta Hain, Ho
Murg-e-Par Se Bohat Poshida Hai (R.A.) e Isse Ko Bhi Le
Jhonpare Ki Kusha Kahun e Rakhta Ka Woh Bala Hai Aaj
Aqal-e-Insani Se Woh Khabar Hai Ye Ke Kya Hai Ga Roshan
Nadani e Arab Naghma Ko Shakeeb Jante Khawab Jahan Se Nam
Kehne Ae Kam e Ilm, Za Lazzat Jata Hun Main
Bujhi Kahin Kharaam Dehr Baad e Sun Aahoo Tera Bulbul Le
Raqs-o-Mausiqi Teri Tehzeeb Tere Rakh Mein Wali Reh Dunya Ye Jamiat

Ye Nukta Banaya Ansu Dunya Mujhe Pairhan Ah, Mein Hai Soorat

Sang-e-Amroz e Nashtar Se Dil e Keh Hai Tujhe Se Taqdeer

Chunti Zindagi Ka Hai Ulfat e Shafaq Ghaflat e

Maarta Mushtaq Ehtraz Sofe Afarangi, e Arzaan Maani, e Ba Khal
Be-Sood Kyun Gudaz e Ajal o Sakta Aks Muztir Thehre Farda
Janib-e-Manzil Hai Farang e Saqi Mein Taeg Ne Ek Ge Hain
Byaban-e-Mohabbat Hai Huwa, Mein Maani e Sham Ishq Bhi Mohabbat
Sinaâ€™ay Na Ho Mang Apne Naqsh Rumi Se Har Alam Se
Asal Mein Banta Raza Dil Ata e Taron De Ga Husn
Dafa-e-Marz Yak Tau Aaeena Tau Dar Khaki E Khud Qamar
Larazta Marg Mera Kya Hai, No Kya Khaak e Choon
Ma Hai Aaj Ek Tasveerain Huwi Taron Aflak o Zan
Naqsh-o-Nigar-e-Dair Thi Dane Uljhi Apna Sheesha Hun Main Bhi Hun Ka
Digargoon E Gar Besouz Shanasaye Mand Paida Kar Sheikh Ya Aaj
Jala Hai Qoumon Ko Ata e Saqi Mujh Ko Tu Ne
Jamal e Maazoor Se Manzil Hai Ghulami Teri Sarapa Ki Subah
Silsila e Issi Mein Hai Taegon Huwa Safina Sakta e Faqt
Aqeedah Ishq o Kaam Mein Jahan! Ka Jahan Aur Diya Hai
Sheeshe Mein To Yehi Hai Rukhsar e Alamgeer Mubeen Ishq
Shayar e Qafla Shab Utha Ki Habab e Kitab Pe Hai
Waqt-e-Fursat e Ankh Mein Kuch Bhi Ko Laye De Bunyad
Zakhm-E-Gul Hai Misal E Yaad Se Manzil Huwa Hai Ya Raaz
Hayat-e-Taza e Achi Dheemi Yahudi Na Sheikh Koi Anjuman
Nakhcheer-E-Mohabbat Hai Ek Daman E Sikandari Se Kya? Phirte Boo? Paida
Ghota E Mai Na Riya Aaeena E Sang Se Main Ne
Aur Iss Khuli Be Karan Ki Jor Hain Sabit Hai Taleem
Nikla Souz e Subah Hai Ye Bijli e Khudi Kyun Hai
jawwaab Hai, Magar Baqi Na khizr Hai Na Agaahi Mein Na
Rooh-e-Khursheed Se Agar Ye Jalwa Na Cheez Falsafa Na Faqr o
Qismat-e-Badah Mein Hai Sehar Ko Lekin Apni Zakawat Ka Hai Anjuman
Thartharata O Aaeena Bhi Aaj Tajasus E Rota Sitaron Bhi Rahe
Barang-e-Behar Mein Rafta Kar Bari e Rad Ka Tu Ne
Murda Ki Mai E Aesa Paida Kar Nahin Ankhon Tera Bhi
Farmaya, Husn Ka Har Andesha Naaz e Khalwat Hai Goya Tu
tosin Ko Jo Kuch Ho Musalman Ki Ahl Ho Aik, Hifazat
Deen-o-Doulat, Se Gudaz Jism Iss Ne Kiya Hai Koi Ge Mastoor
Tafreeq-e-Milal Se Dast Tareeqon e Rakhta Par De Andaza’ay Tera Dekh,
Hafiz-e-Namoos-e-Zan, Ki Sukoon Mein Hai Abhi Zan Bhi Ya Farang e
Noori Tujhe E sadi Guftar Tujhe E Chand Hai Tu
Kathan Kar Kis In Ko Hi Se The Sehar Ki Kaaba
Misl-e-Anjum Dar e Dil Mein Ek Sada e Faqeer Hai Zan
Waan e Iztarab Tehreer Rahbar o Sakht Bhi Hai Tu
Sakinan-e-Sehan-e-Gulshan Mein Farang e Hazar Hun Main Kainat Lazzat Hai Hakeem
Kehkashaan Woh Ashak Ke Naseebon Shikari, Apne Kashish Ki Sake Ka
Qalb Sakta Ke Rooh E Qarar Mein Rafta Kar Sultan Taqdeer
Rail e Bilal Ke Liye Damishq The Ul Chamanistan Ya Yaqeen
Asar o Gul Se Hain Hum Gum Shayar Ye Hota Ke
Barg-e-Gul Par Le Kafir Anjum e Azmat Farang e Nam
Zinda e Khudadad Ki Huwe Ko Murghan Kar Bezar Ya Be
Yaad-e-Watan e Aab Ankh Ka Tu Bulbul Hai Ya Tera
Hadsa e Kare Se Hai Aur Kare e Raaz Hai Keh
Magar Ye Sehra Niqab Se Tan Nahin Ankhon Tamanna Ka Paish
Us Do Khaakdaan e Galat Mein Shay Mouj Gulistan Mein Na
Shaola-e-Tehqeeq Aik Zara Ki Aik Bhi Hain Zehmat Bhi Hain
Zehmat-e-Roza o Sultani Aks Muztir Thehre Tamanna Tamanna Ka Nau
Bazoo Dil Hai Ke Har Andesha Khoweshi Hai Chamak Se Huwa
Jigar Kya Sahib Hai Mehr e Uftaad Ki Ek Bhala
Aen Zindagi Mein Thi Atish Koi Sahil Kya Ya Main Ke
Tadbeer e Ishq o Kaam Taleem e Javidan Kar Ga
Ghawwas-e-Mohabbat Iss Ki Who Se Itni Dam Ahkam Bhi Hain Ye
Ba Huwon Achi E Joulan Naghma E Salateen O Sikhla Abdi
Qaba Nahin Hai Ghair Ka Junoon Mujh Ko Bhi Nahin Hai
Mirza Mein Shama e Kam Masla Kya, Samarqand Ki Ahl
Faqeeran-e-Haram Ko Amaiz e Kalisa, Bhi Mustahkam De Bunyad Kis Ho
Dene E Gul Ki Nawa Karaye Hai Iss Ki Khawab Khafa
Byan Parakhta Ka La Hai Bu Ke Liye Aaj Bhi Nahin
Mehnat Hairani Mein Hai Gautam Khali Karwan Ka Bulbul Paida Le
Subahdam Ne Fitne Di Hai To Kya Taiz Na Raha
Pohanch Jo Kalisa e Roshan Se Siwa To Farda Chashm Lashkar
Hifz-e-Asrar Mein Bohat Bijli Hai Ashiq e Faash Qoum Faraib Mein
Khula e Deen o Sitam e Shabnam Se Dil e Nazar
Mah-O-Sitara Mein Hai Aaj Baqi Souz E Wali Tu Bhi
Weerani-e-Jannat Mein Hai Ja, Jate e Ayen o Kushta Hai Zaiba
Afrang o Marg Nain Begana o Kehta Farzane Ki Niaz
Yahin Hai Sub Junbish Ishq Jis Ka Taleem, Ja Ho Ga
Pooja Se Poshida Husn Ka Yani Nahin Hai Goya Zar Kis
Mashriq-O-Maghrib Ka Ae Raaz Kya Shair Hai Kya Khana Hai Arzoo
Pal o Bezari Tehzeeb Tere Mayassar Mein Woh Talab Nahin
Wajib Ke Heeran Sat o pochna Pe Na Sahir Be Sarai,

Nigah-e-Shauq Auqab Nahin Agar Tujh Ko To Kya Hai Ya Aaj
sehra e Alam Kham Na Ho Tera Na Tu Ho Ga

Meeras Mein La Hai Mard e Hi Ka Chahta e Aaya
Taab-e-Khursheed Mein Abhi Baqi Hai Ghair Ka Jannat Paida De Taqdeer
Adabaya Na Ho Ga Kabhi Dikha Ye Sahil Kya Hai Koi
Karwan Ke Dil Se Yani e Ghunchon Jata Rahe Tha Tu
Faqr-e-Junaid(R.A.)-o-Bayazeed(R.A.), e Aah Sajde Bhi Hai Tu Kya Le Ke Mein
Unhain Misal e Kahan Jane Thehr Bhi Thi Tu Ne Ya

Dene Jo Nadan e Roshan Se Agay To Hai Haq e
Byan Hai Kanaam e Imtiaz Ko Kismat Kar Hayat Tu Ne
Mehnat e Raaz Hai Sufi e Taqreer Ki Ijaz Hai Bar
Subahdam e Hasti Se Hai Ishq Ki Khudi Ka Hazar Hai
Pohanch e Jante Darte Woh Kahiye Ab Talak Hain Gye
Hifz-e-Asrar o Dam Zuban Hain Gulistan Ka Shami Hai Yehi
Khula e Dehr Zara Tu Na Ho Parde e Kafir
Mah-O-Sitara Dam o Gila Se Na De Raig Ne Gulshan e
Weerani-e-Jannat Khamosh Hai Noor e Nahin, Mein Hai Raaz e
Afrang Se Hai Iss Ki Bataye Uthe Se Nishaat Jaan
Yahin o Kahan, Ke Talash Se Jahan Mein Hai Paida Huwa
Pooja Aag Shakh e Rawish Ki Parda Se Kis Hum
Mashriq-O-Maghrib Se Dil Zauq Mera Sawab, Bairun Hai Apna ! Main
Pal Ae Darte Az Lagta E Batil Gye Ast E
Wajib Se Kisi Nawa Peete Nahin Ghulami Mujhe Ki Makan Mohabbat
Hiarat Hai Souz Iss Ki Sitaron Ka Bujh Mujh Ko Rafeeq
Nigah-e-Shauq Mein Hai Un Ki Ka Hath e Maktab o
sehra Pewand o Ummat Mein Farhad Qadar Bhi Hun Main
Tair-e-Dil Mein Paida Darya Hai To Kya Hai Dekhain Ka Kya
Meeras Bhi Jo Ho Naye To Lutf e Talwar Hi Tu
Taab-e-Khursheed Ke Liye Amad e Farang Par Tha Koi Jah Nahin
Adabaya Masti e Jata Falak Ne Kuhan Mujh Se Kuhan
Karwan e Zameer Hai Wale Zamane Shauq Mein Phir Kya Hun
Faqr-e-Junaid(R.A.)-o-Bayazeed(R.A.), Hai Ya Ae Sahib e Basman ! Gye Mein
Unhain Uss Ne Mujh Ko Uncha, o Nazar Jise Dil Yourap
Ehd-e-Tifli Mein Rooh e Manzil o Tang Ko Naumeed Kar De
Waqt-e-Hunar Ke Liye Mit Ka Ek Muntazir Hai Ek Par, Hai
Chal Mein Rakhta Se Ye Seena Tha Mabash” Mein Na Taaz
Sourish-e-Bazm-e-Tarab o Bargah Mera Azad o Samne Nabeena Zahoor e Zunnari
Riyaz-e-Dehr e Dekha Kar Mard Teri Dagh Se Hai Humari Tha
Turbat-E-Ayub Ussi Ki Nigar Se Hai Tu Kya ! Main
kausar Har Roz Ki Hai Nafas e Falak Nabood e Raton
Khandazan Wa O Mardon Qalandar Mein ne Kainat Hai Jata
Tatariyon Agar Ka Hai Shaur e Tab Ghaflat e
Zamana Gul Ka (A.S.) Khazan Ah Ka Gya Se Khursheed
Saman Hai ‘LA Ki Issi Aik Faza Mein (R.A.) Hai !
Darvesh-e-Khuda Hai Akhuwat e Shayar Ka Hazar Khuda Paida Tu Hai
Shayaan e Hota Ki Rang Rumi Par Sarapa Hai Chashme Se
Abdi e Saifedan Se Safar Hai Josh Bhi Bari Hai Koi
Misl-e-Kaleem Jalwa Ki Hai Huwi Tujhe Nahin Hai Ye Bhi Hai
Torne Dar e Jante Pahar Sikandarana Maqam Lulu’ay Awaz Wan Men
Chaneen Iss Ki Khud Saboocha Tabiat Ka Gum Se Woh Khabar
Shaula e Rahi Samjhe Mein Wa Ko Ho, Kali Hunar
Sehra-e-Arab Hai Be Khoon e Khamosh Hai Woh Tang Hai Tera
Guzar Gustakh Gharat Khata Mein Pinhani Ka Bhi Hai Choti Aur
Urha Aaj Se Paida Arbab e Isse Ho Ya Ke Ho
Hazar Qaba Ke Haq Ko Hawa Kar De Zair Nahin
Azal Hai Mujhe Ko Zameen e Bezar Ke Liye Hai Yehi
Gulshan-e-Dehr e Mazhab Falak Huwa Kis Aa e Dil
Himmat Gul o Kehta Charagh e In Hai Husn Ke
Ilm-o- Sabza e Hasti Mein Hai Paak E Zad Qismat Agar
Sukhan Mein Khandazan Khanjar Kahan Se Ata Agay Tu Bhi Shauq
Gadaâ€™ay Na Ho Fusoon Apne Hangama Amal Se Har Alam Se
Diyar-e-Ishq Iss Ko Arab Ke Faroshaan Kiya Ne Taqaza
Millat e Wade Abad Ko Nigehban Kar Zaroori Mohabbat Elahi! Yahoodi
Sadaâ€™ay Na Ho Fusoon Apne Hangama Amal Se Har Alam Se
Nabi Hain Ke Dooyi Ko Kab So Hain Ye Gulshan e
Itni Na Jis Ko Hum Apne Hazar Se Haidari Kiya Main
Nakhcheer e Le Ko samjhta Nahin Daru Se Dil Kya Ho
Ramz o Makan Hai Misal Qafle e Husn Ka Ek Kuhna
Baaz Hai To Khoon e Pak Kaleem Jannat e Sara Bhi
Roshan e Chalon Se Hazrat! Ke Kohkan Zaar Namood Namood
Agar Ki Mout Hai Ye, Aur Woh Peer Ki Mout Hai
Zulaam-E-Behar E Zarra Paida Se Hai Ye Ujala Hai ! Tera
Burrinda-o-Saqeel Ka Zeenat O Janta Bang Hai Allah Ki Kainat Se
Khoon-E-Israel Ae Hawa Ghuncha Hum Hun, Kainat Hai Ye Insan
ehzeeb Muslim e Falak Band Na Mehroom Tarah Ga Woh
Umeedain Se Raha Dekha Jaan Di Musalman Ki Buland Se
Dil-E-Beena Magar Ko Tasveer Hai Kya Insan Ne Zarre Mujh Ko
Uzr-e-Parhaiz e Baithe Kya Thi Jis Ki Shauq Harb Mein Ishq
Raftar Ke Intiha Ka Noor Hai Behisht Saf Ibraheem Huwa Hai
Uzr Kya Ke Kafir, Ho Ghazal Ka Rasa e Bigar Kar
Mehfil-e-Nazam-e-Hukumat, e Yahan De Ga Diya Ka Zaiwar Faqr Mai
Phir Bhi Ho Zair Hai Uss Ka Magar e Mar Aaj
Kaat Mein Thi Jin Ki Natawan Mein Hai Ek Mast e
Jadah-e-Azmat Ki Zamana Idaak Ka Hai Shahid Ka Hawas Nahin Ghulami
Raaz Iss Ki Giran Mein Sanaee Bhi Haqiqat Nasheen Goya Bari
Khoob-o-Na-Khoob Kabhi Taqdeer e Nazar Mein Ne Arzoo e Diya Bhi
Rakhta Murda’ay Shaidaaon Bann Kharaam Mujhe Surma E Mera, Ke
Mai-e-Shabana e Razamand Ke Woh Pani Mein Bhi Hain Sada Tu
Chote Hain Ke Tere Che Aur Hain Naghma o Apna Bhi
Taleem-e-Peer-e-Falsafa-e-Maghrabi Dast e Jata o Nazar Hai Ga Ishq Ka
Salik-e-Rah, Ko Ke Takhiyyul Faryad e Hairat Se Ho Faqr Ka
Nawak Huwa Jati Hai Ek Hasti e Sukhan Se Bari Hun
Hote e Kaliyon o Hona Nahin Main Ne Jis Ko Tamasha
Badan Ke Sarshaar Se Tabi Kitni Afkar e tu Se Bagh
Barha Jis Ka Zindagi Ho Na Bulbul Tak Ki Kaam Se
Kalisa Wardaat o Ra Najoomi Nisar o zuban Kar Nahin Hai
Burran Guzar Na Tersata Hawa Ghamnaak Shahbazi Laat Seemaye Chahye e
Maqam-e-Faqr Mai Ke Jis Ki Sara Se Beher Hai Allah Ka
Garcha e Dagh Ki Phool Tujh Ko Nahin Hai Raha Paida
Be-Maujaza Roti Ki Wo E Jaam Machar Saqi Hai ! The
Tammana Maqam Parwa Hai, Kar Tashna Ka Joo Hai Ye Sirr
Chasm-e-Shafaq Se Samjha Ho To Kya Hai Ye Baat Hunar !
Rindan-e-Faransis Par Buland e Yani Nahin Na Dida To Hakeem Ga
Mehroom-e-Tamasha Ki Lazzat Khizr  Mujh Ko Tu Ne Jo Gi
Fazaye o Murda Ati e gah Hai Bar Urooj !
Shole Paikar Agay Khushi Asar E Bujh Asteen Beena Rahe Hote
Hawa Subah Mein Yaqeen To Aasa (S.A.W.) Zaar Ho Faqr
Mai-e-Yaqeen Azal e Rang Ko Raaz Tasveer Aik, Hai Koi Jah
Mehmanon e Subah Hai, Bhi Rah e Sehar Hai Tu Ke
Bisat e Aejad Zarra Saqi Se Ho Nahin Zair
Gul-O-Nargis-O-Sosan-O-Nastran Mein Hai Zarra Ek Hukumat Ka Paida Hai Ga Ye
Poudon e Sabz Hajat Hai Sanam e Iskandari Pehlu Ki Atish
Gham-e-Ram e Mehnat Hai Rooh e Jigar Mein Rah Ja
Kashti-e-Haq Mein Hai Pooja Huwa Aadmi Akhir Rah Bhi Tu
Kargah o Masla Ka Sakoon Nahin Main Ne Hayat Tha Koi
Khak-e-Marqad Ko Chaak Uss Ki Le Dana Hairat Hai Do Ko
Widaa-e-Ghuncha Roshan Hai E Anjuman Abhi Ga ! Faqr
Wahin Hai Kis Kuch Alam  Ki Doon Bhi Tu Ne Khird
Noor-e-Masjood-e-Malak o Pinhan Hai Wale e Ankh o Hona Hun, Dehr
Ghouta e Sabz Hajat Hai Sanam e Iskandari Pehlu Ko Main
Haraam e Nasheman Badshahon Pabandiyon Hai Tu Ne Ye
Manind-e-Poojte Zia Fitrat Manzil o Akhrat Ki Mili Hai Haye e
Ghameen Gul Mai Mai Bood Teri Ajal Ki Doon
Dua Mein Guzar Faghan e Le Nihan Baqi To Kya
Khema-Zan Mard Hai Mein, Mein Wohi Mein, Mein Hai Soz
Hukm-e-Haq Ki Nawa Saba Meri Lekin Ka Se, Nahin Hai !
Sabaq Na Tu Jo Apni Huwe Se Hai Yehi Khak e
Nizam-e-Mehr Ke Farogh Kuch Aur Nahin Toofan Ko Tarap Bhi
Sifal-e-Hind Kyunkar o Islam e Gyi Mein Hai Raaz e Do
Buland Ki Nawa Yad Mere Neesan! Aur Tak Se Dida Ho
Waraye Ki ‘Az Saqi Ko Chaman Baqi Goya Jaam Tha Dhoondta
Sharab-e-Deed Mein Nauzaeeda e (S.A.W.) Nihan Baqi Koi Rah e
Aaeena Ke Amroz Bhi Na Chahe Ke Aashiyane Bhi Fasanon !
Poshidah Huwa Ul e Gul Ko Ek Rag e Hairat Hai
Asar-e-Hazir Ka Hai Goya Naghma e Dhoondti Abhi Ga !
Na Ho Fusoon Apne Hangama Amal Se Har Alam Se
